The map tiles are updated based on the \nposition and size of the svg viewBox.\n\nsvg_map(svg_object,{parameters})\n\nThe following parameters can be defined:\n\nTile provider:\n    api_key        : The api key for the tile provider (required)\n    max_zoom       : Maximum zoom of the tile provider (default: 18)\n    min_zoom       : Minimum zoom of the tile provider (default: 0)\n    tile_size:     : Tile size in pixels by tile provider (default: 256)\n\nPosition definitions\n    x       :  Horizontal position of the upper left corner in SVG coordinate space\n    y       :  Vertical position of the upper left corner in SVG coordinate space   \n    width   :  The width (and height) of the map rectangle in SVG coordinate space\n    frame   :   The ID of any SVG object with attibutes x,y and width. This overrides\n                any previously defined x,y,width attributes\n            \nTiling:\n    zoom    :   The initial zoom level\n    zoom_levels    : If set, the available zoom levels will zoom_delay      : How long we freeze old tiles when zooming (default: 1000)\n   \nTodo:  Create event upon zoom-level change\n\n*/\n\n\nfunction svg_map(svg,p) { return new svg_map_obj(svg,p)
